    5046              : /*
    5047              :  * initArrayResult - initialize an empty ArrayBuildState
    5048              :  *
    5049              :  *      element_type is the array element type (must be a valid array element type)
    5050              :  *      rcontext is where to keep working state
    5051              :  *      subcontext is a flag determining whether to use a separate memory context
    5052              :  *
    5053              :  * Note: there are two common schemes for using accumArrayResult().
    5054              :  * In the older scheme, you start with a NULL ArrayBuildState pointer, and
    5055              :  * call accumArrayResult once per element.  In this scheme you end up with
    5056              :  * a NULL pointer if there were no elements, which you need to special-case.
    5057              :  * In the newer scheme, call initArrayResult and then call accumArrayResult
    5058              :  * once per element.  In this scheme you always end with a non-NULL pointer
    5059              :  * that you can pass to makeArrayResult; you get an empty array if there
    5060              :  * were no elements.  This is preferred if an empty array is what you want.
    5061              :  *
    5062              :  * It's possible to choose whether to create a separate memory context for the
    5063              :  * array build state, or whether to allocate it directly within rcontext.
    5064              :  *
    5065              :  * When there are many concurrent small states (e.g. array_agg() using hash
    5066              :  * aggregation of many small groups), using a separate memory context for each
    5067              :  * one may result in severe memory bloat. In such cases, use the same memory
    5068              :  * context to initialize all such array build states, and pass
    5069              :  * subcontext=false.
    5070              :  *
    5071              :  * In cases when the array build states have different lifetimes, using a
    5072              :  * single memory context is impractical. Instead, pass subcontext=true so that
    5073              :  * the array build states can be freed individually.
    5074              :  */
